  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ba1beb2f-c921-4149-84e1-012582bb6ec7'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396343682i/9119736.jpg' alt=' photo 097f74d9-aea2-4f25-bf8d-387e1938aa88_zpscbc96c35.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After reading <i>Lick</i>, I’ve been waiting for this book. For Mal’s book. I loved him in the first and I had such high hopes for his story. Let me tell you... It didn’t let me down! I love rockstar books, but these are in a different league. Not only are they hot, sweet, and full of sexy rockstars, but they are off the charts hilarious. I laughed so hard in this story! But it wasn’t just funny- there was a lot of depth in there too.<br/><br/>Anne is in a pinch. Once again, she’s been u</span>
  <span id="freeText2886896375279473312" style="display:none"><b>5 ‘Crazy Eyes’ stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/097f74d9-aea2-4f25-bf8d-387e1938aa88_zpscbc96c35.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396343682i/9119736.jpg" alt=" photo 097f74d9-aea2-4f25-bf8d-387e1938aa88_zpscbc96c35.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After reading <i>Lick</i>, I’ve been waiting for this book. For Mal’s book. I loved him in the first and I had such high hopes for his story. Let me tell you... It didn’t let me down! I love rockstar books, but these are in a different league. Not only are they hot, sweet, and full of sexy rockstars, but they are off the charts hilarious. I laughed so hard in this story! But it wasn’t just funny- there was a lot of depth in there too.<br><br>Anne is in a pinch. Once again, she’s been used by someone she’s trusted. Her roommate has bailed on her, moving out without paying Anne any of the money she owes her. Anne has responsibilities- bills to pay, along with helping her little sister with college. For one night, her neighbor Lauren gets her to forget about her issues and head to a party with her. At her friend’s Ev and David’s place. <br><br>When Anne gets there, she is feeling a bit out of place. She goes outside and takes a call from her friend, when she stumbles upon Malcom Ericson. The drummer from Stage Dive. Mal see’s Anne and hears her conversation. He loves that she makes crazy eyes at him and wants to help her out. More importantly, he needs her help. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/7d500685-f62b-4657-b9d3-45154f0ba5f3_zpsc93c05b6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396343682i/9119737.jpg" alt=" photo 7d500685-f62b-4657-b9d3-45154f0ba5f3_zpsc93c05b6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mal needs a fake girlfriend for his own reasons. A nice girl, someone to clean up his act and reputation as a ladies man. Who better than Anne? There is something about this girl he likes. So he decides he’s moving in with her after meeting her that one night.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’re moving in with me?”<br><br> “Yes, pumpkin. I am moving in with you.” <br><br>“When did we talk about this exactly?” <br><br>“Actually, you might have left by then. But it doesn’t change the facts.”</blockquote>
</i><br> Mal is the light hearted, fun loving, and a bit crazy drummer. He always has something funny to say, something crazy he’s doing, but deep down, he’s more than that. And Anne sees that. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/e91beb49-3c94-43fe-85be-0875591becad_zpsae46a2b5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396343682i/9119738.jpg" alt=" photo e91beb49-3c94-43fe-85be-0875591becad_zpsae46a2b5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So Anne and Mal living together solves both of their problems. Anne no longer has to worry about paying her rent, and Mal has a sweet and beautiful girlfriend. As long as their convincing and stick to the boundaries they set so things don’t get complicated, everything should be right as rain... <br><br>This book had so many moments of laughter, I lost count. I had a near constant smile on my face. I couldn’t control the laughter! Mal was something else entirely. I adored him and his sense of humor. Anne had her funny moments as well! <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“We’ve broken my bed,” I said, stating the obvious.<br><br>“In battle, sacrifices must be made, pumpkin.”....<br><br> “They’re mocking us,” I said.<br><br>“Nonsense. We just fucked so hard we broke your bed. They wish they were us. The natural order of sexual status has been restored.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Hands down, that’s the most romantic thing I’ve ever heard. I can pretty much feel my legs just falling wide open for you right now.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/d364c815-b19a-4957-9338-9b7bbd210620_zps53ac6668.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396343682i/9119739.jpg" alt=" photo d364c815-b19a-4957-9338-9b7bbd210620_zps53ac6668.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Oh, god, no.” I covered my face with my hands. “Please don’t.”<br><br>“Shh. This is a private conversation.” He brushed hot feverish kisses up and down the lips of my sex. My stomach tensed so hard it hurt. “Look at you all pretty, pink and excited. Don’t worry, I’ll look after you.”<br><br>“If you don’t stop talking to my vagina I’m going to kill you.”<br><br>“You’re beautiful Anne’s pussy. Just beautiful. And I’m not mean like her. I’m on your side and I love you very much.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Whatever you’re imagining, it’s bigger.”<br><br>“I’m not imagining anything.” <br><br>“I’m serious, it’s basically a monster. I cannot control it.”<br><br>“Malcolm...”<br><br>“You’re pretty much going to need a whip and a chair to tame it, Anne.”<br><br>“Stop it.”</blockquote>
</i><br>You see what I mean? So so so funny! <br><br>Even though Mal and Anne were in a ‘fake’ relationship, they really worked together. Not to say there weren’t some difficult moments, but overall they were good together. Their ‘fake’ relationship turned into a real friendship... and real feelings developed. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/0cfbbd98-12d9-4534-a71e-e3549f711206_zps7904b5ff.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396343682i/9119740.jpg" alt=" photo 0cfbbd98-12d9-4534-a71e-e3549f711206_zps7904b5ff.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mal and Anne were both wonderful characters. Both highly entertaining and fun. I loved the way they interacted, how Anne was able to see the real side of Mal that not many do. He is hilarious, handsome and the center of attention always, but he is more than that. Anne has always had to be responsible, always let others walk all over her. Mal showed her that there was another way to live. These two really worked together. <br><br><i>Play</i> kept a smile on my face from start to finish. Full of sweet, sexy, romantic heart warming moments, and too many laugh out loud lines to count, with characters you can’t help but to love, this is a book I would highly recommend. Bring on Jimmy’s book! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/a0f22ee6-0745-43f2-89be-eeded84aead1_zps9d6c8253.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396343682i/9119741.jpg" alt=" photo a0f22ee6-0745-43f2-89be-eeded84aead1_zps9d6c8253.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13967236287319131941"> <b>2 1/2 to 3–I'M A BIT BAFFLED–Stars</b><br/><br/>Looks like I'm in the minority here! <br/>Everyone seems to love this book but me.   <span id="freeText13967236287319131941" style="display:none"> <b>2 1/2 to 3–I'M A BIT BAFFLED–Stars</b><br /><br />Looks like I'm in the minority here! <br />Everyone seems to love this book but me. I didn't dislike it; in fact, I laughed quite often during the course of the story. I must admit, however, that the plot felt a bit random to me. Even as I closed the book, I was still unsure what this story was really about. <br /><br />I LOVED Mal's character in <i>Lick</i> and couldn't wait to read his book. Unfortunately, for me, he ended up being too crazy, too manic, and too over-the-top. I found it difficult to connect to his character, to Anne's character, to her easy acceptance of his crazy behavior, and to their love story. Sadly, this book, its main characters, and the plot perplexed me more than it enchanted me. <br /><br />That said, the one-liners were hilarious and it was obvious the author had a blast writing Mal's character. Plus, I loved getting more of David, Ev, and the band. Though this book didn't fully work for me, I believe most readers will love reading this story. </span>

No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Play, just as previous Kylie Scott’s novel Lick, is <b>fast paced, incredibly sweet</b> and <b>sexy story</b> that literally swept me off my feet. I quickly found myself<b> falling in love with the main characters</b>, the witty banter between them and the fabulous sexual tension that purely rocked! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395176115i/8961358.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I didn’t think it was possible for Kylie Scott to at least matc</span>
  <span id="freeText5784674873229334030" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Play<br><b>Series:</b> Stage Dive #2<br><b>Author:</b> Kylie Scott<br><b>Release Date: </b> 25th March, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Play, just as previous Kylie Scott’s novel Lick, is <b>fast paced, incredibly sweet</b> and <b>sexy story</b> that literally swept me off my feet. I quickly found myself<b> falling in love with the main characters</b>, the witty banter between them and the fabulous sexual tension that purely rocked! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395176115i/8961358.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn’t think it was possible for Kylie Scott to at least match the awesomeness of Lick. But I was strongly mistaken. Not only did I found Play just as awesome as Lick, I think Mal and Anne made David and Eve run for their money.<br><br>Anne Rollins wasn’t a very close friend of Eve , but yet after disaster of a day, Anne found herself being at the party the David Ferris and his wife were throwing. At the same party she’s met Malcom Ericson, Stage Dive’s drummer and her teenage crush. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395176115i/8961359._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When very funny but weird circumstances made Mal move into Anne’s apartment (without her knowing about it, of course) the things between them start to skyrocketing in hot as sin department. Can you imagine how Anne must’ve been feeling when a half naked rock god occopied her apartment and quickly after that her heart? <br><br>Play is definitely a ‘go’ book for all of the rock star romance books junkies. From the start to finish I was bewitched by how simply yet excitingly this book seemed to follow. There wasn’t a single moment that left me bored. Mal was too funny for that. All the things that came out his dirty mouth where not only hilarous (though, I was close to be rolling on the floor from all the laughing I’ve done) but blazing hot too! I was having so much fun I felt like I was flying through the pages. It was fantastic feeling!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395176115i/8961360.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Was Play sexy? Definitely. Was it funny and light read? Absolutely. Is it worth recommending? Are you kidding? Of course it is!<br> <br>Overall, the <b>original sense of humor, great chemistry between exceptional characters and lots of lots laughing out loud moments </b>made me very happy that I had a chance to meet Mal and Anne closer. So yes, you can say<b> I am obsessed with this series! <b><br><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow <div id="review_1784850057" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1784850057" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1784850057?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=damn-this-guy-is-perfect">damn-this-guy-is-perfect</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=jealous-sweet-guys">jealous-sweet-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=likeable-heroines">likeable-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=rock-stars">rock-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=smexy-read">smexy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=adult-romance">adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1784850057" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8181397927191438491"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Life`s a song, Anne. Let's play."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><b>You cannot just simply resist Mal Ericson.</b><br/><br/>I have been so interested to read the Mal's story ever since <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_' title='Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lick</a>. Well who doesn't want to get to know him more? He's such a fun and goofy character and I knew that behind his playful attitude there's a different side of him that we have yet to see.<br/><br/><b>Malcolm "Mal" Ericson</b> is Stage Dive's drummer. He is known as someone who always <i>"plays"</i> around when it comes to women. With his happy-go-lucky lifestyle,</span>
  <span id="freeText8181397927191438491" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Life`s a song, Anne. Let's play."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>5 Stars!</b><br><br><b>You cannot just simply resist Mal Ericson.</b><br><br>I have been so interested to read the Mal's story ever since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_" title="Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">Lick</a>. Well who doesn't want to get to know him more? He's such a fun and goofy character and I knew that behind his playful attitude there's a different side of him that we have yet to see.<br><br><b>Malcolm "Mal" Ericson</b> is Stage Dive's drummer. He is known as someone who always <i>"plays"</i> around when it comes to women. With his happy-go-lucky lifestyle, relationship is certainly out of the picture. But when he met a personal dilemma that requires him to basically snag a pretend girlfriend, he didn't have a choice but to look for the perfect one to act as his girl. Meeting <b>Anne Rollins</b> at Ev and David's party though was a perfect timing. They automatically clicked after a few minutes of flirting. And because Anne happens to have financial troubles, he proposed to meet her needs in exchange of moving with her in her apartment and her cooperation in his pretend relationship scheme. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You're the best boyfriend. Fake or not."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>You can imagine my face while I was reading this book the whole time.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469249474ra/19796484.gif" width="250" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460788581ra/18787216.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were certainly lots of hilarious moments in this book. Mal didn't fail to crack me up with his sexual innuendos with Anne and his crazy exchange and shenanigans with his band mates. Hilarious scenes aside, there was an emotional side to it that made me appreciate its entirety. I loved Mal and Anne's dynamic. While Mal might be a player, his character development throughout the story-- the way he stuck to Anne and basically followed a monogamous relationship, very well pleased me. There was no cheating involved which made me love this book even more. I also loved Anne's character. The way she accepted Mal behind his many layers and the way she stood by him despite the fact the she too has some personal issues was really admirable. This couple is perfect for each other! <br><br>Like most pretend relationship books, these characters fell into a real relationship together, but what I loved about this book was Mal and Anne's mutual acceptance when it comes to their weak sides. Each conflict was immediately resolved without getting into so much drama which I really loved.<br><br>What also made me embrace this book was Mal's relationship with his family, especially with his mom. It was touching. I even found myself crying over some scenes here. I think his family relationship was the one that truly changed Anne's feelings toward her mom, too. <br><br>I also thought the rock star theme here was more palpable compared to the previous book. In this installment there was certainly a lot of stage actions by the Stage Dive. I felt their passion to music because of their performances and connection with their fans.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Mal's playing and the music owned me, the smoothness of his movements and his absolute focus. His energy."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6476625.Kylie_Scott" title="Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">Kylie Scott</a> made it really possible to balance out both the hilarious and emotional vibes in this book. Play, in my opinion, was better than Lick. I loved that it possesses all the elements (sexy times included) to make it a lot more enjoyable. If you've enjoyed David and Ev's story in Lick, then you definitely need to get into Mal's story. <br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <a href="https://pagesofpearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472382775i/20186886._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pages of Pearl" width="400" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    </a>
  </p>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog?shelf=favorite-boys">favorite-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog?shelf=best-cover">best-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog?shelf=want-to-read-soon">want-to-read-soon</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer816709328" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5959761347179162199"> <b>"Life's a song,Anne.<br/>Let's play." </b><br/><br/>Wow I'm a big fan of this series!!I loved Lick and I loved this one!!This book was so refreshing and funny!!I laughed so loud!!Mal is hilarious!I was really looking forward for his book!!<br/><br/><br/>Anne wasn't lucky in her life.She is a good person, she cares for everyone but sometimes people take advantage of her..Her roommate walk out on her and her boss use her.When her friends asked her to go with them in a party, she decides to go with them..and there she will meet th</span>
  <span id="freeText5959761347179162199" style="display:none"> <b>"Life's a song,Anne.<br>Let's play." </b><br><br>Wow I'm a big fan of this series!!I loved Lick and I loved this one!!This book was so refreshing and funny!!I laughed so loud!!Mal is hilarious!I was really looking forward for his book!!<br><br><br>Anne wasn't lucky in her life.She is a good person, she cares for everyone but sometimes people take advantage of her..Her roommate walk out on her and her boss use her.When her friends asked her to go with them in a party, she decides to go with them..and there she will meet the drummer of the rock band Stage Dive, Mal!!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395841117ra/9051134.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Mal is so funny also he is moody and manic!When he met Anne in the party he professes that she is his girlfriend!So they move in together!! And just like that, their crazy journey begins!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395841117i/9051133.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anne gets to see a side of Mal that he doesn't share with many people.. Mal and Anne are steamy together, I loved their interactions.Both have their problems but they try to deal with them!Mal and Anne are not normal, they are complete opposites, which is exactly what makes their interactions so entertaining and this is what I really loved in this book!! While I was reading their dialogues I was giggling and swooning . ;DI loved Mal so much!!I liked that he is a little crazy, he wanted to live in the moment!I think he helps a lot Anne because she is the opposite of him! I loved Anne!She is a strong character a little crazy too :) but also she is lovely!<br> <br><b>"Pumpkin, I'm always serious when it comes to you. Even when I'm messing around, I'm still serious as shit. Whatever you need, whatever I have to do. It's been that way since we met."</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394319282ra/8835922.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kylie does a fantastic job!!I love her writing!!I look forward to reading the rest of the band mates stories!!<br><br><a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer894977772" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2796749561229716135">I loved Book one Lick.<br/><br/>And I loved this book! Even more!<br/><br/>Mal was so much more than he promised in Lick!<br/><br/>Mal and Anne meet at a party, Mal decided he liked Anne, and that he needs Anne (for reasons of his own) and Anne needs him. So he moves in and convinced Anne to be a pretend Girlfriend. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>"You moved in with me somehow".......<br/><br/>"I know what you're gonna say, it's sooner than I thought too. But Davie threw me out today so I figured, why wait?"<br/><br/>I just blinked, the rest of me being too frozen to respo</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText2796749561229716135" style="display:none">I loved Book one Lick.<br /><br />And I loved this book! Even more!<br /><br />Mal was so much more than he promised in Lick!<br /><br />Mal and Anne meet at a party, Mal decided he liked Anne, and that he needs Anne (for reasons of his own) and Anne needs him. So he moves in and convinced Anne to be a pretend Girlfriend. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"You moved in with me somehow".......<br /><br />"I know what you're gonna say, it's sooner than I thought too. But Davie threw me out today so I figured, why wait?"<br /><br />I just blinked, the rest of me being too frozen to respond.<br /><br />"Okay. Long story short, I accidentally saw Ev naked" He held up both hands protesting his innocence. "It was only side boob, I swear...But you know what he's like with her....Not my fault she was topless. Anyway, Davie went ballistic.....Harsh words were said. We may have even wrestled slightly. But I forgive him. Love makes you psycho, right?"<br /><br />......<br /><br />"So you moved in with me?"<br /><br />......<br /><br />"Anne, come on. We talked about this last night. If you were gonna have a problem with me moving in, that was the time to bring it up, not now."</b>
</i><br /><br />And that sets the tone for the book! Mal is a beautifully written character! His humour, his playful nature, his childlike vulnerability that comes through sometimes, his manic energy - all hiding something, a pain you occasionally get glimpses of!<br /><br />And Anne was a great character too. She saw down to the real Mal, behind the famous drummer.<br /><br />Together they were perfection, the chemistry, the banter between them was great.<br /><br />And seeing more of the rest of the band, and how close they all are and support each other was beautiful!<br /><br />It was a funny, sexy, at times a little sad, but hugely enjoyable read, that somehow manages to pass the brilliance of book one!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15046274375119892978"><b>4.5 STARS! ★★★★☆</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“We’ve broken my bed,” I said, stating the obvious.<br/>“In battle, sacrifices must be made, pumpkin.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420728893ra/13255819.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well holy cow! When I first met Mal in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_' title='Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lick</a>, I knew he would be a totally fun guy to read about but I didn't expect how crazy and freakin hilarious this read was! Once I started, I couldn't put it down and I even had to sacrifice a bit of sleep just to read a little bit more of Mal!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“Make love. I meant make love … of course. I would never just stick my dick in you. I would make </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15046274375119892978" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS! ★★★★☆</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“We’ve broken my bed,” I said, stating the obvious.<br>“In battle, sacrifices must be made, pumpkin.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420728893ra/13255819.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well holy cow! When I first met Mal in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_" title="Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">Lick</a>, I knew he would be a totally fun guy to read about but I didn't expect how crazy and freakin hilarious this read was! Once I started, I couldn't put it down and I even had to sacrifice a bit of sleep just to read a little bit more of Mal!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Make love. I meant make love … of course. I would never just stick my dick in you. I would make mad, passionate love to this sweet, sweet body of yours for days, no, weeks. It would be beautiful, pumpkin. There’d be little angels, and birdies, and you know … all just hanging around, watching. Perverts.”</i>
</blockquote> <br>I just loved how I didn't need to take this book seriously AT ALL. Yes it was ridiculous, yes it was OTT at times but damnit I didn't care. This was exactly what I needed in my life right now and although I thought the ending was a little rushed, I'm rounding this read up to 5 stars because let's face it....Mal was damn f*cking awesome. Everything that came out from his mouth was absolutely GOLD! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Pumpkin, stop rubbing your ass against me. We gotta go! I don’t have time to do you now. Prioritize, woman.”</i>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394998728ra/8933740.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm starting to recall right now how awesome rockstar reads are. NEED MORE OF THEM IN MY LIFE! Btw Rachel, I fluffin' love you right now for making me read these! ♥♥ <br><br>Read this series, everyone! READ IT IF YOU LOVE EM' ROCKSTARS!!! *peace out*</span>

Normally I buffer my dirty reads with another genre, but after enjoying Mal’s cameos in the first book so much I couldn’t stop thinking about him. Also, he was a drummer . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>As I powered through this puppy without coming up for air.<br><br>Alright, so the story is obviously about Mal the drummer . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

However, <i>something</i> about him has been a bit off lately. <br><br>Meet Anne – she’s Ev from Book #1’s former next-door-neighbor who returns home from work one day to find her roommate has hightailed it out of Dodge and left her with little furniture and zero rent. <br><br>When the two meet at one of David and Ev’s parties, the story comes out and Mal decides to fix things . . . . by moving in and paying Anne’s debts in trade for her pretending to be his girlfriend. It was exactly what I look for in a romance – not too long, not too angsty (and the angst that was featured was worth getting all emo over), plenty of laughs, and likeable characters. I mean seriously likeable. I never thought anyone could replace Miles Archer as my number one fantasy man, but Mal did a pretty effin’ good job . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Highly recommended. We’ll see if I continue on with this series. I’m not real interested in Jimmy or Ben’s characters so I’m putting it on the backburner until someone convinces me to change my mind.<br><br><b>ORIGINAL "REVIEW"</b>:<br><br>I planned on breaking free of the porny spiral and reading something else, but who the hell am I trying to kid?         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer891649649" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6566363149698748895"><strong>Book</strong> – Play (Stage Dive #2)<br/><strong>Author</strong> – Kylie Scott<br/><strong>Publication Date</strong> – March 25, 2014<br/><strong>Type</strong> – No Cliffhanger Series<br/><strong>Genre</strong> – Romance/Humor<br/><strong>Rating</strong> – 5 out of 5 Stars<br/><br/><em>Complimentary Copy provided by Author (Release Blitz) in exchange for an honest review.</em><br/><br/><strong>Review</strong><br/>First things first….OMG OMG OMG…..I WANT MALCOLM!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395884474ra/9057793.gif' alt='' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*whew…OK….now that’s out of my system – I can continue on with my review – what a fucking fantastic book…we had EVERYTHING all wrapped up in a cute story….we had an abundance of humor, a strong heroine, </span>
  <span id="freeText6566363149698748895" style="display:none"><strong>Book</strong> – Play (Stage Dive #2)<br><strong>Author</strong> – Kylie Scott<br><strong>Publication Date</strong> – March 25, 2014<br><strong>Type</strong> – No Cliffhanger Series<br><strong>Genre</strong> – Romance/Humor<br><strong>Rating</strong> – 5 out of 5 Stars<br><br><em>Complimentary Copy provided by Author (Release Blitz) in exchange for an honest review.</em><br><br><strong>Review</strong><br>First things first….OMG OMG OMG…..I WANT MALCOLM!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395884474ra/9057793.gif" alt="" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*whew…OK….now that’s out of my system – I can continue on with my review – what a fucking fantastic book…we had EVERYTHING all wrapped up in a cute story….we had an abundance of humor, a strong heroine, a fucked up hero, a love triangle, a life changing incident, black-eye, broken bed, crazy eyes….all of these pulled at every emotion in me….but the one emotion I treasure the most is the laughing!! <br><br>Malcolm stole the show in this book….I hate to compare authors….but this one really reminded me of a character in Tara Sivec’s books – he was my favorite there…..and Malcolm is my favorite in this series.  I really don’t know how you are going to top him Ms. Scott….but then again after reading Lick – David was my favorite…so you might just surprise me yet!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395884474i/9057794.jpg" alt="" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to share with you a post from our BR thread – because Wendy swears it sums up the book -<br><br><blockquote>
<br>This is one fucking fantastic book - Even better than Lick - Hands down Malcolm is my favorite in the Stage Dive Band members....you never know if he is serious or joking around.</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395884474i/9057795._SY540_.jpg" alt="" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>I kinda thought the reason why he wanted Anne to be his pretend girlfriend was because of someone in his family wanting him to settle down....but for the book being so funny throughout...this is making my eyes water thinking about how sensitive and caring Malcolm really is.<br> <br> Yeah - I got pissed at him when he forgot about Anne and was up on that skank...but then I loved how he dealt with Reese. Yes, he saw how Anne was being taken advantage of by her "so called" friends and Malcolm built up her self-esteem in order for her to create boundaries with others.</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395884474i/9057796._SY540_.jpg" alt="" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two are most adorable couple and Anne wins hands-down the feisty, comical uber strong character. She knew from the beginning what she was getting in to and she didn't let that bring her down. She thought she would be left high and dry when the band went on tour...but still she gave it shot - putting her "future hurt heart" on the back-burner and lived in the "now".<br> <br> I absolutely love this author....I love her style of writing - it's like she has the characters speaking directly to you - instead of telling a story line by line...I feel like I am part of their conversation. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395884474i/9057797.jpg" alt="" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><strong>Re-Cap</strong><br>Everyone is worried about Malcom……Annie just had her “so called” friend leave her high and dry without a penny.<br><br>Annie is forced to go to a party with her next door neighbor who is friends with Ev (from Lick) and the members of Stage Dive.  There, she goes to take a call from her crush “Reese” (the man whore) and Malcolm who is hiding in the shadows hears the full conversation.  He banters with her to the point of getting her so frustrated with him that she tells him directly where to go (even though she has lusted after his posters since her teenage years).<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395884474ra/9057798.gif" alt="" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The next day Malcolm shows up at her apartment all moved in with a great plan.  She pretends to be his girlfriend and he will pay off her rent.  Annie knows this is a bad idea given her lusty feelings toward Mal but agrees thinking it may just be what will set Reese off to finally settle down.<br><br>Annie gets more than she bargained for spending time with Mal – he makes her laugh, he makes her angry and he makes her live again.<br><br>I have to stop here…because there is no way that I am giving away the book…you will just have to read it for yourself – you will not be disappointed!<br><br><strong>For more reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong> <a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394342368i/8839977._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo banner_zps637f7ed8.jpg" width="400" height="70" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_760546714" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/760546714" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/760546714?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer760546714" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18246464775573769551"><b> 4.5 laughing my ass off stars </b><br/><br/>I. FREAKING. ADORED. THIS. BOOK!!!!!!!!!!<br/><br/>For those of you who haven’t caught onto the Stave Dive series, which starts with the brilliant first book Lick, get on it now!!! Warning, this review will be told mostly in quotes because I could never replicate the awesomeness that is Ms. Scott’s writing style.<br/><br/>Play is the story of Mal, the playful drummer of Stage Dive, and Anne, the charming and cute girl who works in a book shop. The story starts when Anne is screwed ove</span>
  <span id="freeText18246464775573769551" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 laughing my ass off stars </b><br /><br />I. FREAKING. ADORED. THIS. BOOK!!!!!!!!!!<br /><br />For those of you who haven’t caught onto the Stave Dive series, which starts with the brilliant first book Lick, get on it now!!! Warning, this review will be told mostly in quotes because I could never replicate the awesomeness that is Ms. Scott’s writing style.<br /><br />Play is the story of Mal, the playful drummer of Stage Dive, and Anne, the charming and cute girl who works in a book shop. The story starts when Anne is screwed over by a friend who basically steals a bunch of money (not literally) and leaves Anne in the dust, causing Anne to face imminent eviction. After meeting Mal at a party, and a slightly infuriating conversation, Anne finds Mal moved into her apartment the next day, and a proposal she cannot turn down. Mal will front Anne the money and live with her, and she will pretend to be his girlfriend (for somewhat mysterious reasons).So we’ve all heard this plot before right? Whatever. Ms. Scott puts a creative spin on an old idea and truly makes it her own.<br /><br />Why did I love this book? I had a giant freaking smile on my face the entire time I was reading it. The banter between Anne and Mal is hilarious, and their chemistry even better. Here are a series of quotes from the book to prove my point:<br /><br /><i> <b> “We start fucking and you’ll be all ‘Oh Mal, I never dreamed such ecstasy was possible. I cannot live without you. Fuck me, Mal. Pleeeeease.’”<br /><br />“His gaze rested on a young woman browsing in the True Crime section. You’d have thought he’d have enough sense to turn away when she picked up a book on female serial killers, but no.”<br /><br />“What do I taste like?” <br />“Well like honey and cream and… I dunno, bread?” <br />I scrunched up my nose. “Bread?” <br />“Yes, sexy bread that I could eat all the time because you are so delicious and full of whole grain goodness.”<br /><br />“It would be beautiful, pumpkin. There’d be little angels, and birdies and you know… all just hanging around watching. Perverts.” </b> </i> <br /><br />While this book had it’s funny side, it also had serious moments that gave me all the feels. Anne accepted Mal for who he was and never expected him to be anything more than that. In return, Mal wanted to build something with Anne and did his best to make her happy.<br /><br /><i> <b> “Don’t have sad eyes, Anne. I can’t fucking stand it when you’re sad.”<br /><br />“You’re good for me. You take me any mood I come in. I don’t have to be always happy or on around you. You roll with any shit I say and give as good as you get. You don’t let me push you around if it doesn’t suit you and you haven’t asked me to buy you a fucking thing.” <b> </b></b></i><br /><br />So, needless to say Kylie Scott is now on my mental list of authors to automatically buy their books.<br /><br />Why not a full 5 stars? The story felt a bit unfinished, I would have liked to know what Anne is doing with her life, kind of like how Evelyn decided to keep working in hers and figure stuff out. Maybe it was my late night reading and I missed it, but Anne’s path in life (the parts not including Mal) seemed a bit vague.<br /><br />Also, and everyone please put the pitchforks down when I say this, but for me, this is what I expected from the Sinners on Tour series. This series blows that one out of the water. (Please don’t attack me! I still love the Sinners).<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.wordpress.com/2014/04/04/play-by-kylie-scott/">http://rachelsreadsravenously.wordpre...</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="18246464775573769551" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11909319939718264503">4 'I love you, Mal' stars!!!!<br/><br/><b> <blockquote> He spun on his heel to face me, arms out wide. “Life’s a song, Anne. Let’s play.” </blockquote> </b><br/><br/><blockquote> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469867979ra/19865683.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> </blockquote><br/><br/>After reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_' title='Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'> Lick</a> I was hooked but while reading 'Lick,' I fell in love with Stage Dive's drummer, Mal.   <span id="freeText11909319939718264503" style="display:none">4 'I love you, Mal' stars!!!!<br><br><b> <blockquote> He spun on his heel to face me, arms out wide. “Life’s a song, Anne. Let’s play.” </blockquote> </b><br><br><blockquote> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469867979ra/19865683.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br>After reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_" title="Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener"> Lick</a> I was hooked but while reading 'Lick,' I fell in love with Stage Dive's drummer, Mal. So, when I found out the second book was his story I nearly died of a heart attack and couldn't wait to continue to fall for the hilarious Mal. <br><br>In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19095025.Play__Stage_Dive___2_" title="Play (Stage Dive, #2) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener"> Play</a>, we have Anne. Anna gets ditched by her bitch of a 'friend' leading Anna being roommate less, moneyless and practically homeless. Anna was in a hell of a situation, but that wasn't going to stop her from going to a party she was invited to. And yes, the party was no other than Ev and David Ferris' house party <i> (I didn't realize how much I missed them until they had little scenes! <b> *sad face* </b>)!</i> Anne, was a fan of Stage Dive and had the biggest crush on of course my boyfriend, Mal <i> (seriously who doesn't?)</i>. The only thing was that, her attending that party indeed ending up changing her life, forever. <br><br><b> <blockquote> “The point of me telling you my name, even when you already knew it, was so you’d give me yours. That’s how these things go.”<br>“You knew I knew?”<br>“The crazy eyes kinda gave it away.”<br>“Oh.”<br>A moment later, he groaned. “Never mind, this is taking too long. I’ll just make one up for you.”<br>“Anne.”<br>“Anne, what?<br>“Anne Rollins.”<br>A brilliant grin lit his face. “Anne Rollins. See, that wasn’t so tough.” </blockquote></b><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443625970ra/16387066.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The party changed her life in much more ways than one. The biggest one was the fact that Mal gave Anne a deal, and the deal was for her to be his fake girlfriend and in exchange, he will pay her rents and anything else she needed. Anne was nothing more than baffled that her last long crush wanted her to be his fake girlfriend but Anne wasn't dumb, she knew something was up, and she was willing to take the deal but also try and figure out why Mal wanted her as his fake girlfriend.<br><br><blockquote> <b> “Yes, pumpkin,” said Mal, his face deadly serious. “I am moving in with you.”<br>I cringed at the horrid nickname but chose to focus on the real concern for now. “When did we talk about this exactly?”<br>“Actually, you might have left by then. But it doesn’t change the facts.” </b>
</blockquote>  <br><br><br><i> Side Note: </i><br><blockquote> <b> Dear Mal,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469871098ra/19866260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Anne is a sweetheart and a helper. All her life she's always had to be an adult and take care of her mother and her younger sister. She's strong, independent, witty, worries a lot but also knows how to go with the flow. She's someone I could see myself being friends with in real life <i> (clearly wouldn't happen because she took my man). </i> But, what made me adore her was the plain fact that she wasn't a typical whiny heroine and that she stood by Mal's side through their downs. She handled every situation maturely and wasn't petty whenever she was angry or hurt. She said what was on her mind and managed everything as it came.<br><br><blockquote> <b> “Promise me something,” I said.<br>“Sure.”<br>I stopped, smiled. “You didn’t even hesitate.”<br>“You’re pissed about something.” He leaned down, making our conversation private despite the packed room. “What’s wrong?”<br>“Promise me you won’t sleep with her.” I nodded to the beast in question.”<br>“I won’t sleep with her,” said Mal.<br>“And you won’t have sex with her either.”<br>He rolled his eyes.<br>“Just to clarify.”<br>“What’d she do to you, Anne?”<br>“She insulted me. But it’s fine.” I just needed to know she’d never get near him. Now my soul was at peace. “Carry on with your partying.” </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463984345ra/19180917.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br><b> Mal.. </b> my crazy lovable don't take too seriously Mal. He was the highlight in 'Lick' for me and to be completely honest I was going to rate this a '3.5', but Mal (&amp; David) are the reason why it was bumped up to a 4. I felt like the author didn't write this story to its full potential and it gets me a tad bit mad because, it's MAL but looking past that, I still adored the hell out of this story. Mal, made my heart melt and had me rolling on the floor with every crazy thing he said. We get to see Mal's problems get told, and I just want to hold him because when Mal's sad, I'm sad. I'm happy he had someone like Anne by his side. OH! Before I forget! What I loved about Mal in this story was the fact that we got to see his serious &amp; jealous side. I was surprised to see it during this story because I just couldn't see Mal being serious or jealous but both of those sides were sexy.<br><br> <blockquote> <b> The slow curl of his lips made something hot and delicious unfurl deep in my stomach. <br>“Pumpkin, I’m always serious when it comes to you. Even when I’m messing around, I’m still serious as shit. Whatever you need, whatever I have to do. It’s been that way since we met. Haven’t you noticed yet? We’re fucking destined or something. I can’t help myself. It’s pathetic, really.” </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464440605ra/19239289.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br>Now let's talk about Mal &amp; Anne together!?!? They had me smiling and laughing the whole book. They balance each other out in every way and that's why they just meshed together. Anne was everything Mal wasn't, and Mal was everything Anne needed. I LOVE the fact that Anne was able to change Mal's moods and have him going crazy for her, and I LOVE how Mal allowed Anne to live life and loosen up. What they needed all their lives were each other. What they had was inspiring and heart warming AND hilarious. <br><br><blockquote> <b> “I FUCKING LOVE YOU, ANNE.”<br> “Yeah, okay. Shut up now.” David tried to slap a hand over Mal’s mouth. “AAAAAAANNNNNE!” My name was a long, drawn-out howling kind of noise, muffled at the last when David managed to cover his mouth. Muted grunts and snarling came next. <br>“God damn it,” swore David. “He just fucking bit me.” <br>“My love shall not be silenced!” </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469870023ra/19865986.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br><b> Oh my god. Oh my god. </b> Can we talk about David for a second????? Whatever I'm going to anyways! I promise on everything I did not expect to miss David and Ev until they showed up in the story. He and Ev play a good amount of role in the story, and I'm so happy they do. I knew they'd appear in it but I thought it would be 'hi' &amp; 'bye" type appearance but NOPE, they were in a lot of scenes being cuter than life itself. You even get to STILL see how much they are in love and how much David truly loves Ev <i> (fuck it, I'm rereading 'Lick')</i>.<br><br><blockquote> <b> "Love you, baby.” David kissed her back. “Love you too.” He whispered something in her ear. Something that made her giggle. <br>“We can’t–my parents are here. Later.” <br>David’s mouth turned downward. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469870242ra/19866052.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br>That's another reason why I was going to rate this story a '3.5' because my mind kept switching to wishing it was Ev &amp; David's story (I know I felt like I was cheating on Mal but David is still my husband so...). I LOVE how David was still a bad ass and Ev was still a darling. David appears a lot in this story because  of course he's David, and he can do what he wants - he's Mal's best friend and just like Mal was there for David in 'Lick', David was there for Mal even though David wanted to punch Mal a few times. Their bromance is probably the cutest thing I've ever read, and I say that confidently. Mal, felt lonely because his best friend was married but no matter what, David was there for him even at his darkest times. <br><br><blockquote> <b> I pulled out my phone then hesitated. Ev had pissed me off, holding me up, but these people were also his family. They deserved to know he was still in one piece. </b> <br><br><i> Anne: He’s at the practice hall<br>Ev: Thank you </i><br><br><b> David Ferris strode in not fifteen minutes later. He nodded to me, then picked up a guitar and plugged it in. As the first strains of noise rang out Mal opened one eye and saw David standing opposite him. Nothing was said. Time moved by, both sluggish and swift at once. The two of them played for hours. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405714557ra/10440826.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br>All in all, this was a fast read for me since I can't get enough of Mal and his humor. I'll probably end up rereading this in a few weeks and end up giving it '5' stars to be completely honest with you. Even though I've only read 2/4 of the books in this series, I am HIGHLY recommending everyone to read it! This book will have you laughing your head off at every single page, and I promise you that. Give it a try and thank me later <b> (no but seriously, thank me later because I know you will) ;)</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425064589ra/13839669.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more reviews! <br>Click below :)<br><div> <a href="https://bookitwithdon.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465508902i/19367462._SX540_.png" alt="Book It With Don" width="275" height="140" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a> </div></b></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Rock Fans, Kylie Scott fans, Everyone</span></div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer891881762" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3858902158443886141">5 I Don't Care, I Keep Reading Great Books Stars * * * * * <br/>Buddy Ready with my Angel Carol, Woot Woot<br/><br/>I have been on a roll... I have read all types of books with one thing in common... They have been Fucking GREAT. Some have been more serious, more intricate; others have been a lark or hot and steamy.<br/> <br/>What all of them have in common is fantastic writing. <br/><br/>I am talking about writing which makes you care; which makes you think of nothing but the words in front of you. You want to be part of the sto</span>
  <span id="freeText3858902158443886141" style="display:none">5 I Don't Care, I Keep Reading Great Books Stars * * * * * <br>Buddy Ready with my Angel Carol, Woot Woot<br><br>I have been on a roll... I have read all types of books with one thing in common... They have been Fucking GREAT. Some have been more serious, more intricate; others have been a lark or hot and steamy.<br> <br>What all of them have in common is fantastic writing. <br><br>I am talking about writing which makes you care; which makes you think of nothing but the words in front of you. You want to be part of the story and climb through the e reader or pages and become one with the book. Doesn't matter what the specific story is about... it is the craftsmanship of the author and how they tell the story which causes this reaction.... and I have had a run of them.<br><br>Kylie Scott is one of those authors. My first experience with her was through a little book called Lick. I found it on my own... read it on my own and enjoyed it that way, too. I was oblivious of any hype or push. Just knew what I liked; filed it away and that was that. I found out recently there was a follow up called Play happening. Since I read for a blog as well as for myself now, I am fortunate to be able to read early. This was the case with Play.<br><br>This book did not disappoint. Ms. Scott has remained true to her talent and voice. There was a smooth embrace with her words; a sense of ease where everything just fit. The humor was so perfect it couldn't have been timed any better. There were also moments of humor laced with a sadness which worked devastatingly well, too. Those moments gave us insight to see this wasn't just a piece of fluff... it had heart, meaning and would make us think.<br><br>And think I did... as the main character seemed to be an enabler... but not in the positive way which can enhance a relationship... no it was in the way others can repeatedly take advantage of them. We get to see how our girl realizes she has the right to say no and look out for herself. What is delicious is how our male lead shows her the way.<br><br>So thank you Ms. Scott for remaining true to your talent and giving me another wonderful read full of heart, life; yes, extremely steamy and sexy times and strong story. 5 Stars? Hell yes... <br><br>A gifted copy was given by the author/publisher in exchange for an honest review<br><br><strong>For more reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_692589053" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692589053" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692589053?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692589053" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer645125723686175587">After meeting Mal in the first book, <i>Lick</i>, I could hardly wait to get to know this sweet and funny drummer <i>better</i>...much better. And I was not disappointed...well, maybe just a tad. <br/><br/>Mal is everything you think he is...fun, crazy, wild and your typical rock god manwhore but there's something going on with him. It's almost like he has ADD.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396387767i/9126519.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And right from the moment he meets Anne and wants her as a "fake" girlfriend, you just know there's something going on. Especially because he sets rules...rules </span>
  <span id="freeText645125723686175587" style="display:none">After meeting Mal in the first book, <i>Lick</i>, I could hardly wait to get to know this sweet and funny drummer <i>better</i>...much better. And I was not disappointed...well, maybe just a tad. <br><br>Mal is everything you think he is...fun, crazy, wild and your typical rock god manwhore but there's something going on with him. It's almost like he has ADD.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396387767i/9126519.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And right from the moment he meets Anne and wants her as a "fake" girlfriend, you just know there's something going on. Especially because he sets rules...rules such as no sex. What? That's right, no sex! <br><br>Mal has been Anne's fantasy since she was young and had his posters all over her walls so when he makes her the offer, she would be crazy to turn him down. She decides to let herself enjoy everything there is since it's not real and just have fun. Little did she realize that she couldn't control her emotions. <br><br>It certainly doesn't help when she decides to give Mal some of his own medicine and claim his kisses don't affect her. It only makes Mal more determined to kiss <b>
  <u>the daylights out of her</u>
</b> but she is not complaining. ;)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396388407ra/9126579.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mal and Anne are great together though...the perfect Yin to his Yang. ;) And while it takes a bit to get to the actual deed, there are sooo many great and funny "pretend" scenes that it ~sort of~ makes up for it. The bed scene...priceless! <br><br>Naturally, there's tons of scenes with the other band members which I loved. I can't get enough of David and Ev...they are so cute together. There's also some interesting moments with Jimmy and Lena and Ben and....(I'm not really going out on a limb here but yes, I'm calling it....) <b>LIZZY</b>. (It will happen whether Anne likes it or not...LOL)<br><br>Of course there's drama...drama in the form of one of Mal's prior hook ups (tsk tsk Mal), Anne's wanna be boyfriend, Reece (who is also a manwhore), Anne's family and Mal's family. It was all rather interesting but for me it lacked the emotional intensity that was in the first book. I wanted to see the <b>
  <i>real</i>
</b> Mal and while I'm glad we didn't get to suffer through the details of that particular drama, it still left me feeling a bit bereft. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396387866ra/9126527.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I did enjoy how things ended up and certainly "Killer" was a nice touch as was the epilogue. Maybe a longer book would've been more satisfying. <br><br>Anyway, I'm definitely looking forward to Jimmy's book, <i>Lead</i>, which comes out July 29th and of course Ben's, <i>Deep</i> which is scheduled for December 23rd. <br><br><br><b>
  <u>Recommendation:</u>
</b><br><br>A great series if you enjoy rock stars that have more of a story going on than just sex. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396388248ra/9126568.gif" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “So, I’ve given this absolutely no thought and decided that you need boundaries, Anne. Boundaries. Are. Your. Friends.”<br><br>♥ “Your shirt is on inside out, child bride,” said Mal, the side of his mouth kicking up. “What have you been doing?”<br><br>♥ “There go the crazy eyes again,” he whispered.<br><br>♥ “Please don’t call me that.” <br><br>“Puuuumpkin.”<br><br>♥ “Life’s a song, Anne. Let’s play.”<br><br>♥ “You read too many books.” <br><br>“No such thing!” I cried, aghast.<br><br>♥ “We’ve broken my bed,” I said, stating the obvious. <br><br>“In battle, sacrifices must be made, pumpkin.”<br><br>♥ “You’re the best boyfriend ever. Fake or not.”<br><br>♥ "Anne, you might diss my kissing but I’m telling you now, my oral sex skills are off the chart. I know all about getting dirty down under. Let me show you, pretty please?”<br><br>♥ “Sweetie pie? Pumpkin? You screamed so loud my ears are still ringing. I can’t actually hear whatever bullshit you’re peddling right now. Tell me later after I get a couple of stitches put in my shoulder, okay?”<br><br>♥ “Pumpkin, I’m always serious when it comes to you. Even when I’m messing around, I’m still serious as shit. Whatever you need, whatever I have to do. It’s been that way since we met. Haven’t you noticed yet? We’re fucking destined or something. I can’t help myself. It’s pathetic, really.”<br><br>♥ “Hello, Anne’s clitoris. It’s me, Malcolm, your lord and master.” <br><br>“Oh, god, no.” I covered my face with my hands. <br><br>“Please don’t.” “Shh. This is a private conversation.”<br><br><br><b>**Thanks to Melissa, Patty, Denisse and Jennifer for the BR!**</b></span>

<div id="review_1084800416" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1084800416" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1084800416?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084800416" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16176436348013234971"><b>5 <i>Sexy Mal</i> Stars</b><br/><br/>Anne Rollins has always done whatever she could to help people she cares about. She quit school to take care of her sister and mother, she covered her roommates half of rent and utilities when she lost her job, and she allows her boss and guy she has been crushing on for two years use her as a back up plan when his actual dates fall through. So when the rockstar she has had a crush on for years asks her to be his girlfriend, there really is one answer…where do I sign up. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414350674i/11643427.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, so</span>
  <span id="freeText16176436348013234971" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>Sexy Mal</i> Stars</b><br><br>Anne Rollins has always done whatever she could to help people she cares about. She quit school to take care of her sister and mother, she covered her roommates half of rent and utilities when she lost her job, and she allows her boss and guy she has been crushing on for two years use her as a back up plan when his actual dates fall through. So when the rockstar she has had a crush on for years asks her to be his girlfriend, there really is one answer…where do I sign up. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414350674i/11643427.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, so no quite. Anne immediately taken back by Mal’s request and really can’t take him seriously. I mean this guy wants to move in with her and have her be his pretend girlfriend. This is absolutely crazy, but she is at risk of being evicted after her roommate bailed on her past due rent and utilities. While it is hard to take Mal seriously and she isn’t aware of his motivations, Anne agrees to go along with his crazy plan. <br><br>Her new sexy rockstar roommate/fake boyfriend definitely makes things interesting. <br> <br><b>
  <i>“Whatever you’re imaging, it’s bigger.”<br><br>“I’m not imagining anything.”<br><br>I’m serious, it’s basically a monster. I cannot control it.”<br><br>“Malcom..”<br><br>“You’re pretty much going to need a whip and a chair to tame it, Anne.”<br><br>“Stop it.”</i>
</b><br><br>Mal had me laughing my ass off. He is one of the funniest characters I have ever read. He is funny in that is he serious kind of way and honestly sometimes I am not sure myself. <br><br>Yet, as you get to know Mal it is easy to see there is more to him then he lets on. Something is haunting Mal. So of course, I always feel like I can solve this mysteries, so I start guessing. The natural guess is drugs, I mean he is a rockstar. Is he trying to prove he can be good boyfriend material to another girl. Is he sick, bored, lonely?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414350674i/11643428._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mal and Anne begin things with their fake relationship, but the longer they live together the harder it is to keep things platonic. They decide to add a little bit of sexy time to their relationship..you know to make things more believable. <br><br><b>
  <i> "You’re beautiful Anne’s pussy. Just beautiful. And I’m not mean like her. I’m on your side and I love you very much.”</i>
</b><br><br>So first comes fake relationship, then comes hot sex, then comes a real relationship. The more they get to know each other, they develop real feelings. Mal loves that Anne isn’t with him for fame or fortune and always knows how to handle him. Anne loves that Mal accepts her boundaries, wants her to stand up for herself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414350674i/11643429.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I absolutely loved this story. I especially loved Mal. I loved his sarcasm, he had me laughing out loud, gasping, and even talking to myself about how crazy he is. I also loved how sexy he was, how he sees Anne for who she is and takes up for her, how he protects her. Anne was a great heroine, there were times I wanted her to do things differently, but I think she was more realistic then me, since I would be jumping to be with Mal Ericson. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Life could be strange and beautiful thing sometimes.”</i>
</b></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=oregon">oregon</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer881618272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16605379555599530584"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Take a chance, Anne."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><b>Mal</b> caught my attention in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_' title='Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lick</a> and I've been looking forward to his book. The other night my husband and I were watching an Iron Maiden concert/tour on Paladia and I got this HUGE urge for a <i>Rock-n-Roll</i> book. <br/><br/>Mal is known to be the life of the party and when he overhears a personal phone conversation of <b>Anne's</b>, who is down on her luck...Mal proposes the idea of being in a <u>fake</u> relationship with him. Weathering the highs and lows of this whirlwind relationship t</span>
  <span id="freeText16605379555599530584" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Take a chance, Anne."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><b>Mal</b> caught my attention in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_" title="Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">Lick</a> and I've been looking forward to his book. The other night my husband and I were watching an Iron Maiden concert/tour on Paladia and I got this HUGE urge for a <i>Rock-n-Roll</i> book. <br><br>Mal is known to be the life of the party and when he overhears a personal phone conversation of <b>Anne's</b>, who is down on her luck...Mal proposes the idea of being in a <u>fake</u> relationship with him. Weathering the highs and lows of this whirlwind relationship taxes both of them.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I just pick up the next one, keep going, never miss a beat. That's how we roll. Sh*t gets broken, no matter, play on."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Loved that this book was set in Portland, Oregon. Adding books to my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy?shelf=oregon" rel="nofollow noopener">Oregon</a> shelf makes my day. This shelf is dedicated to any book that mentions Oregon or is set in Oregon. <br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21442559.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_" title="Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1394634379s/21442559.jpg" alt="Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19080006.Play__Stage_Dive___2_" title="Play (Stage Dive, #2) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">
