Malcolm!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396654046ra/9167509.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You're so funny<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396654954ra/9167729.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And so sexy<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396654954ra/9167730.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, and Anna? I like you<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396654954ra/9167731.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because how can you not like someone so good, sweet and witty. Besides, she's my namesake, it's natural we clicked from the beginnig. Don't even get me started on Mal. I haven't met such lovely character for a while now. He is CAF, adoringly impulsive, funny, sexy, caring and loving boyfriend, but what impressed me the most was his sincerity.<br>I. Loved. This. Book. <br>It had no drama, only the good stuff. So if you want to read something hilarious, light, sweet and heart melting, add it to your TBR asap!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396654046i/9167510._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <b>"I am, Malcolm, Lord of the Sex!"</b>

It's rare that someone boasts and is absolutely right, but I think in this case...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491078681i/22374274.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Chuck Norris can spot awesomeness.   <b>"Do I need to know her name?"<br><br>"I've heard it helps."<br><br>"Maybe for you," Mal scoffed. "I just call out my own name during sex."</b>
</i><br><br>He meets Anne, who is financially screwed because her roommate skipped out on her, owing her a ton of money. Malcolm is also a super nice guy, so he decides he will "help" Anne out of her financial problems in the best way ever.<br><br>Anne, arriving home from work: <b>
  <i>"You moved in with me somehow....<br>Um, how did you get in again, just out of interest?"<br><br>"Is this going to be an issue?" he asked with a long winded sigh.......<br>"Plus, I'll open jars and lift heavy shit. I hear those are issues for women."</i>
</b><br><br>Oh, Mal? I have a jar that needs to be opened. Don't mind my giant, burly husband. He works a lot.<br><br>Anne has been crushing on Mal since she was a teenage girl with posters of him and the band covering her bedroom walls. She has been porny daydreaming about him for ages. She agrees to be his fake girlfriend for a while in return for his help with the rent. Why does he want a fake girlfriend when he could have any girl on the planet, including slightly chubby older housewives who may be happily married?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491078681ra/22374275.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You'll find out later.<br><br>Anne and Mal actually made a really cute couple. He is hilarious and crazy, she is a little uptight, but also pretty funny. The fact that Mal has made it this far in life without some sort of babysitter is pretty impressive, but he really does need one. And, Anne really needs to let go and have some fun. Plus, she gets to have her teenage heartthrob! It's a great message for teen girls everywhere: Go follow your favorite band around the world. Don't worry about school or work because if you can get his attention, he will fall in love with you and pay all your bills forever. It's a sure thing!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491078681i/22374273.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <span id="freeText17009283575356087207" style="display:none"><b>4 Rocker Stars!</b><br><br>Anne is Eve’s friend (you surely remember her from the first book) and she is currently through a rough phase and is low on money. One night she goes to a party in Eve’s house and she meets her rocker crush, Mal. <br>Mal is the drummer of Stage Dive, a true rocker star: bad boy and playboy extraordinaire.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396050903ra/9083126.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mal’s public image isn’t on his best days, so when suddenly he becomes Anne’s roommate somehow he ends up hiring her to pretend to be his girlfriend and help clean his image.     <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692749985?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=insta-love">insta-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=happy-for-now-ending">happy-for-now-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=laughed-my-ass-off">laughed-my-ass-off</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692749985" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10569103529339470511">4--<b>PLAY-ful</b>--Stars!!<br/><br/>I actually ended up liking this one a lot more than I thought I would. Mal really grew on me. He was funny and quirky and so sweet. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395611038ra/9019997.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The humor was just shy of being OTT. <br/><br/>I'm not a huge fan of this storyline....the relationship built on lies of sort. Pretending to be boyfriend/girlfriend knowing one or both parties will start to have more feelings. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395833015ra/9050128.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Anne needs money. Her roomate bailed on her, took her furniture and left her broke and desperate. She meets Mal at a Stage Dive par</span>
  <span id="freeText10569103529339470511" style="display:none">4--<b>PLAY-ful</b>--Stars!!<br><br>I actually ended up liking this one a lot more than I thought I would. Mal really grew on me. He was funny and quirky and so sweet. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395611038ra/9019997.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The humor was just shy of being OTT. <br><br>I'm not a huge fan of this storyline....the relationship built on lies of sort. Pretending to be boyfriend/girlfriend knowing one or both parties will start to have more feelings. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395833015ra/9050128.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anne needs money. Her roomate bailed on her, took her furniture and left her broke and desperate. She meets Mal at a Stage Dive party and it's like a collision course...fast and furious.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383836438ra/6680615.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mal won't take no for an answer. Anne will be his "pretend" girlfriend and within days he's moved in with her. The story was rather predictable I thought but it was still entertaining. <br><br>It's obvious something is going on with Mal. But both Anne and Mal are locked up tighter than a prison. Neither one wanting to open up to each other.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396300614ra/9113516.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lines get blurry...things become less and less pretend and more and more real....and eventually the truth comes out. Will Anne and Mal be able to face it together or will it bring them down? <br><br>Overall, I enjoyed this one. I laughed and I really did love Mal, OTT crazy and all. There wasn't a bunch of drama and angst. Just a fun, sexy read. I definitely recommend if you're a fan of the series. </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer892399150" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11852742979351223221"><b>4 fun stars!</b><br/><br/>Mal was a standout in the first book. So although the first book didn't quite meet my expectations, I was excited for Play because of Mal. <br/><br/>At first, I wasn't quite sure about how Mal and Anne got together and honestly, I wasn't quite sure if Mal was right in the head or not. But as I read on, I totally got into the groove of the story and ended up laughing hysterically at both Mal and Anne. <br/><br/>Mal is still crazy but crazy in a good way. I actually liked how fleshed out his character was</span>
  <span id="freeText11852742979351223221" style="display:none"><b>4 fun stars!</b><br /><br />Mal was a standout in the first book. So although the first book didn't quite meet my expectations, I was excited for Play because of Mal. <br /><br />At first, I wasn't quite sure about how Mal and Anne got together and honestly, I wasn't quite sure if Mal was right in the head or not. But as I read on, I totally got into the groove of the story and ended up laughing hysterically at both Mal and Anne. <br /><br />Mal is still crazy but crazy in a good way. I actually liked how fleshed out his character was. Same with Anne, who I wasn't quite sure of at first. But just like Mal, she grew on me and I enjoyed her deadpan humor, which is a perfect foil for Mal's more boisterous one. I thought they were perfect together. <br /><br />The humor, the characters, the straightforward low-angst plot made this book a wonderful read for me. It was exactly the type of book I needed at the right moment. <br /><br />Recommended? Hell, yes!!<br /><br /><br /><i>ARC provided by the publisher through NetGalley!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="11852742979351223221" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_892685288" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/892685288" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/892685288?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854239" href="/book/show/19080006-play">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer892685288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2266721813013407233"><b>4.5 STARS!!!!!!!</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/fab51e757745eb01fb408073b14bc328.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285103i/9110734._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo fab51e757745eb01fb408073b14bc328.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Kylie Scott has done it again!!!!</b> I just LOVE these books!!! And I love the name of the band… <i>STAGE DIVE</i>… because that is exactly what it feels like falling for it’s fabulously flawed, talented, and gorgeous band members!!!! <br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/2aa22bf223196793b825a908710f323d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285103i/9110735._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 2aa22bf223196793b825a908710f323d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This one, Play, features <b>Malcolm Ericson</b>, the band’s drummer…life of the party…Nordic god… enigmatic man-whore. I haven’t quite come up with the right word to describe him yet. But he is definitely one of the most unique char</span>
  <span id="freeText2266721813013407233" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS!!!!!!!</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/fab51e757745eb01fb408073b14bc328.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285103i/9110734._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo fab51e757745eb01fb408073b14bc328.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Kylie Scott has done it again!!!!</b> I just LOVE these books!!! And I love the name of the band… <i>STAGE DIVE</i>… because that is exactly what it feels like falling for it’s fabulously flawed, talented, and gorgeous band members!!!! <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/2aa22bf223196793b825a908710f323d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285103i/9110735._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 2aa22bf223196793b825a908710f323d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This one, Play, features <b>Malcolm Ericson</b>, the band’s drummer…life of the party…Nordic god… enigmatic man-whore. I haven’t quite come up with the right word to describe him yet. But he is definitely one of the most unique characters I’ve come across in a while. He is a tall… and gorgeous blonde who lives by his own rule book, that apparently no one else can understand.<br><br><b>
  <i> The depth to which he didn't give a fuck was actually a large part of his charm. I'd never met anyone like him.</i>
</b><br><br>He loves women… and likes a variety… because apart from his mother and his sisters, he’s apparently he’s never been seen with the same one twice. <br><br><b>
  <i> “Do I need to know her name?” “I’ve heard it helps.” “Maybe for you,” Mal scoffed. “I just call out my own name during sex.”</i>
</b><br><br>His manner is strange, and abrupt. And you never know whether he’s being sincere or sarcastic. Although, regardless of his tone, he will always tell you he’s being truthful… <br><br><b>
  <i> “Mal, I can barely tell when you’re being serious as it is.” He rolled onto his hands and knees, then crawled over to me, eyes full of mischief. “If I’m talking to you, I’m serious.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/87d074df-3088-4c77-9ad1-3f4bac75e361.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285103i/9110736.jpg" alt=" photo 87d074df-3088-4c77-9ad1-3f4bac75e361.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And he is always a bit over-confident in regards to himself… in a charming sort of way…<br><br><b>
  <i> “You can’t look away from my luscious half-naked body. The minute I opened the door you were pawing at me. It was like you were in heat or something.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/a5d74f19b72e3b87708139a5fe8f27c2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285103i/9110737._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo a5d74f19b72e3b87708139a5fe8f27c2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then there’s <b>Anne Rollins</b>, Lauren and Nate’s quiet mannered next-door neighbor. Whose roommate has just up and left her with a couple of months of un-paid rent, and a half empty apartment. Anne is a sweet girl who was eager to please..her friends, her boss Reece, who she’s had a crush on now for two years, the same boss who flaunts his womanizing ways in her face, likely knowing how she feels about him. And she is always bending over backwards to please others, and usually getting trampled on in return. <br><br><b>
  <i> “You, Miss Rollins are a doormat.”<br>“I am not a doormat,” I growled, everything in me rebelling at the idea. Either that or running in fear of it…<br>He rolled his eyes. “C’mon, you know you are. It’s right there on your face.”</i>
</b><br><br>Lauren and Nate, at finding Anne at home in her newly vacated apartment had forced her to come along with them to a party at Ev and her new rockstar husband’s home… where she is quietly discovered by the band’s drummer…and her idol… Mal Ericson. And something about her just clicks into place for him… and it is insta-love… or is it insta-‘prentend’ love?<br><br><b>
  <i> "If only my heart would stop slipping into cardiac arrest at the sight and sound of him. It would make things a lot easier."</i>
</b><br><br>After overhearing her telephone conversation, he interjects himself into her life and her problems, forcing his opinions, and pissing her off. He is arrogant and abrupt, but in a sweet kind of way that has her caught completely off-guard, and she doesn’t quite know what to make of him. And this perplexing man throws her off even more when she finds he has moved into her apartment unannounced the following day when she returns home from work. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/7a81cf2f8f5906179e4e738df643933a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285103i/9110738._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7a81cf2f8f5906179e4e738df643933a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then he asks her to be his <i>fake girlfriend,</i>? What?!!!<br><br><b>
  <i> When I opened my eyes, Mal smiled back at me serenely. The arrogant jerk. So confident. So hot. And so damn shirtless.</i>
</b><br><br>This story is quite unique. And just going through it again in my head for this review, has me wanting to go back and read it all over again. It is clever. And the verbal banter between the characters is absolutely fabulous. The quotes… too numerous to recall them all.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/812687_127020_48bb6ebf45_p.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396285564i/9110841.jpg" alt=" photo 812687_127020_48bb6ebf45_p.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> "Why do you never believe anything I say? Anne, I am very serious."</i>
</b><br><br>Mal’s character is so bizarre. You can seriously see her dilemma in the story. Not knowing if she can trust him. Not knowing whether she should allow herself to feel anything for him. And not being able to prevent it when she knew she’d fallen for him. And she does, and she falls hard. Because she finds something in him that is so much deeper on the inside than anyone would have guessed.<br><br><b>
  <i> "Life's a song, Anne. Let's play."</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Animated%20gifs/tumblr_m3rb8jYLlW1r6u5tro1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396285103ra/9110739.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m3rb8jYLlW1r6u5tro1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> "You know you can be kind of intense sometimes, Malcolm Ericson." He watched me in silence. "You come across as this happy-go-lucky type dude most of the time, but you are in fact a man of many layers. You are kind of complicated."</i>
</b><br><br>LOVE LOVE LOVED this book. The only reason I didn't give it a fifth star was because I thought the ending was too abrupt. I was hoping for a little more at the end. Who knows maybe we’ll get a bit more of these two in the next book… <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19286623.Lead__Stage_Dive___3_" title="Lead (Stage Dive, #3) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">Lead</a>, which will be Jimmy’s book… SQUEEEEE!!!! Can’t wait!!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2266721813013407233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('v0U5MR9PeEfEgd9s+zkK4DdUtooLsgUrWnleHVunKCtO4gAr1pXS9w+o1XacBPx+o19yn+R53rsIGLTG+MDxvA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eH22yOqb+xpP7qp8a83AybxcE+/TcftzgdUzYOrWu4eJ2o/SI0FRqoTHoGYM8DZXKFfX+jy6IOPTtNm7SbFiEA==')})
  }
